    { 4178;    ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012812;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF ServiceIndexMethod <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                 FILTERGROUP(2);
                                 SETRANGE("Service Index Method", ServiceIndexMethod);
                                 FILTERGROUP(0);
                               END;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ContractAmountsbyDate@1100528600 : Record 11071708;
                                  NewContractAmount@1100528601 : Decimal;
                                BEGIN
                                  LastAmount := 0;
                                  NewAmount := 0;
                                  LastIndexDate := 0D;
                                  Msg := '';
                                  IF UpdateContractAmount THEN BEGIN
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE(Type, ContractAmountsbyDate.Type::"Service Contract");
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Service Contract No.", "No.");
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Service Object No.", '');
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETFILTER("Index Date", '<=%1', ReferenceDate);
                                    IF ContractAmountsbyDate.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
                                      LastAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate."Amount (LCY)";
                                      LastIndexDate := ContractAmountsbyDate."Index Date";

                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETFILTER("Index Date", '>%1', NewIndexDate);
                                      IF NOT ContractAmountsbyDate.ISEMPTY THEN
                                        Msg := Text002;
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Index Date", NewIndexDate);
                                      IF NOT ContractAmountsbyDate.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                                        ContractAmountsbyDate.FINDFIRST;
                                        IF NOT OverwriteExisting THEN
                                          Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text003, Text013)
                                        ELSE
                                          Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text003, '');
                                      END;

                                      ContractAmountsbyDate."Index Date" := NewIndexDate;
                                      NewContractAmount := LastAmount * (100 + ContractAmountPerc) / 100;
                                      IF RoundContractAmount <> 0 THEN
                                        NewContractAmount := ROUND(NewContractAmount, RoundContractAmount)
                                      ELSE
                                        NewContractAmount := ROUND(NewContractAmount, 0.01);
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.VALIDATE("Amount (LCY)", NewContractAmount);
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate."Index Percentage" := ContractAmountPerc;
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate."Round Amount" := RoundContractAmount;
                                      IF Finalize THEN
                                        IF NOT ContractAmountsbyDate.INSERT(TRUE) THEN
                                          IF OverwriteExisting THEN
                                            ContractAmountsbyDate.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                      NewAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate."Amount (LCY)";
                                    END ELSE
                                      Msg := Text005;
                                  END;

                                  IF Finalize THEN BEGIN
                                    "Last Index Date" := NewIndexDate;
                                    MODIFY;
                                  END;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No.,Status,Blocked,Customer No.,Service Index Method,Last Index Date }

               DataItemTable=Table11071707;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Service Contract No.,Line No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT UpdateInstallmentAmount THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                               SETFILTER("Ending Date", '%1|>=%2', 0D, NewIndexDate); //kzwerver, 131031, n, #C007771
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ContractAmountsbyDate@1100528600 : Record 11071708;
                                  NewInstallmentAmount@1100528601 : Decimal;
                                BEGIN
                                  LastAmount := 0;
                                  NewAmount := 0;
                                  LastIndexDate := 0D;
                                  Msg := '';
                                  IF UpdateInstallmentAmount THEN BEGIN
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE(Type, ContractAmountsbyDate.Type::Installment);
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Service Contract No.", "Service Contract No.");
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Service Object No.", '');
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Installment Line No.", "Line No.");
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETFILTER("Index Date", '<=%1', ReferenceDate);
                                    IF ExcludeNegativeInstallmentAmts THEN
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETFILTER(ContractAmountsbyDate."Amount (LCY)", '>%1', 0);
                                    IF ContractAmountsbyDate.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
                                      LastAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate."Amount (LCY)";
                                      LastIndexDate := ContractAmountsbyDate."Index Date";

                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETFILTER("Index Date", '>%1', NewIndexDate);
                                      IF NOT ContractAmountsbyDate.ISEMPTY THEN
                                        Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text002);
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Index Date", NewIndexDate);
                                      IF NOT ContractAmountsbyDate.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                                        ContractAmountsbyDate.FINDFIRST;
                                        IF NOT OverwriteExisting THEN
                                          Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text004, Text013)
                                        ELSE
                                          Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text004, '');
                                      END;

                                      ContractAmountsbyDate."Index Date" := NewIndexDate;
                                      NewInstallmentAmount := LastAmount * (100 + InstallmentAmountPerc) / 100;
                                      IF RoundInstallmentAmount <> 0 THEN
                                        NewInstallmentAmount := ROUND(NewInstallmentAmount, RoundInstallmentAmount)
                                      ELSE
                                        NewInstallmentAmount := ROUND(NewInstallmentAmount, 0.01);
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.VALIDATE("Amount (LCY)", NewInstallmentAmount);
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate."Index Percentage" := InstallmentAmountPerc;
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate."Round Amount" := RoundInstallmentAmount;
                                      IF Finalize THEN
                                        IF NOT ContractAmountsbyDate.INSERT(TRUE) THEN
                                          IF OverwriteExisting THEN
                                            ContractAmountsbyDate.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                      NewAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate."Amount (LCY)";
                                    END ELSE
                                      IF ExcludeNegativeInstallmentAmts THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP
                                      ELSE
                                        Msg := Text006;
                                  END;

                                  IF ShowErrors AND (Msg = '') THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Service Contract No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 9257;3   ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table11071743;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Line Type,Code,Belongs to Scheme,Index Date)
                                 ORDER(Descending)
                                 WHERE(Line Type=CONST(Object),
                                       Expired=CONST(No));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               SETRANGE("Index Date", 0D, ReferenceDate);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  MaintenanceSchemeVersion@1100528601 : Record 11071743;
                                  SubcontractorService@1100528603 : Record 11071789;
                                  MaintenanceManagementCU@1100528600 : Codeunit 11012829;
                                  NewSchemeVersionAlreadyExists@1100528602 : Boolean;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF SubcontractorFilter <> '' THEN
                                    IF SubcontractorService.GetSubcontractorByLevel(
                                      "Service-Contract"."No.", "Contract Object"."Service Location No.", Code, "Belongs to Scheme", '', '', 0, SubcontractorFilter) = ''
                                    THEN
                                      CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF (LastMaintenanceHeader."Line Type" = "Line Type") AND (LastMaintenanceHeader.Code = Code) AND (LastMaintenanceHeader."Belongs to Scheme" = "Belongs to Scheme") THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  TmpIndexedMaintSchemeVersion := "Maintenance Scheme Version";
                                  IF NOT TmpIndexedMaintSchemeVersion.FIND('=') THEN BEGIN
                                    TmpIndexedMaintSchemeVersion.INSERT;

                                    Msg := '';
                                    IF "Index Date" > NewIndexDate THEN
                                      Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text002, FIELDCAPTION("Index Date"), TABLECAPTION);

                                    NewSchemeVersionAlreadyExists := MaintenanceSchemeVersion.GET("Line Type", Code, "Belongs to Scheme", NewIndexDate);
                                    IF NewSchemeVersionAlreadyExists THEN
                                      IF NOT OverwriteExisting THEN
                                        Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text009, TABLECAPTION, Text013)
                                      ELSE
                                        Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text009, TABLECAPTION, '');

                                    IF Finalize THEN BEGIN
                                      IF NewSchemeVersionAlreadyExists AND OverwriteExisting AND ("Index Date" <> NewIndexDate) THEN BEGIN
                                        MaintenanceSchemeVersion.DELETE(TRUE);
                                        NewSchemeVersionAlreadyExists := FALSE;
                                      END;
                                      IF NOT NewSchemeVersionAlreadyExists THEN
                                        MaintenanceManagementCU.CopyMaintHeaderAndLines("Maintenance Scheme Version", NewIndexDate, MaintenanceSchemeVersion);
                                      IF NOT NewSchemeVersionAlreadyExists OR OverwriteExisting THEN
                                        MaintenanceManagementCU.IndexMaintLinesViaHeader(MaintenanceSchemeVersion,
                                          AddActMaterialPerc, AddActLaborPerc, AddActSubcontrPerc, AddActPlantPerc, AddActSundryPerc, RoundAddAct);
                                    END;
                                    LastMaintenanceHeader := "Maintenance Scheme Version";
                                  END ELSE
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF ShowErrors AND (Msg = '') THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Code=FIELD(Object No.),
                            Belongs to Scheme=FIELD(Maintenance Scheme) }

    { 6681;1   ;DataItem;ContractObjectPriceAgreement;
               DataItemTable=Table11071702;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Service Contract No.,Service Object No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT UpdatePriceAgreementAmount THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ContractAmountsbyDate@1100528600 : Record 11071708;
                                  NewPriceAgreementAmount@1100528601 : Decimal;
                                  UpdateByPrice@1100528602 : Boolean;
                                BEGIN
                                  LastAmount := 0;
                                  NewAmount := 0;
                                  LastIndexDate := 0D;
                                  Msg := '';
                                  IF UpdatePriceAgreementAmount THEN BEGIN
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE(Type, ContractAmountsbyDate.Type::"Price Agreement");
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Service Contract No.", "Service Contract No.");
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Service Object No.", "Service Object No.");
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Installment Line No.", 0);
                                    ContractAmountsbyDate.SETFILTER("Index Date", '>%1', NewIndexDate);
                                    IF NOT ContractAmountsbyDate.ISEMPTY THEN
                                      Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text002);

                                    IF FORMAT("Index Interval") = '' THEN BEGIN
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE(Type, ContractAmountsbyDate.Type::"Price Agreement");
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Service Contract No.", "Service Contract No.");
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Service Object No.", "Service Object No.");
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Installment Line No.", 0);
                                      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETFILTER("Index Date", '<=%1', ReferenceDate);
                                      IF ContractAmountsbyDate.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
                                        LastAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate."Amount (LCY)";
                                        LastIndexDate := ContractAmountsbyDate."Index Date";

                                        ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Index Date", NewIndexDate);
                                        IF NOT ContractAmountsbyDate.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                                          ContractAmountsbyDate.FINDFIRST;
                                          IF NOT OverwriteExisting THEN
                                            Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text014, Text013)
                                          ELSE
                                            Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text014, '');
                                        END;

                                        ContractAmountsbyDate."Index Date" := NewIndexDate;
                                        ContractAmountsbyDate.CALCFIELDS("Currency Code");
                                        UpdateByPrice := ContractAmountsbyDate.IsQuantityBasedOnContractObject AND (ContractAmountsbyDate."Currency Code" = '');
                                        IF UpdateByPrice THEN
                                          NewPriceAgreementAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate.Price * (100 + PriceAgreementAmountPerc) / 100
                                        ELSE
                                          NewPriceAgreementAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate."Amount (LCY)" * (100 + PriceAgreementAmountPerc) / 100;
                                        IF RoundPriceAgreementAmount <> 0 THEN
                                          NewPriceAgreementAmount := ROUND(NewPriceAgreementAmount, RoundPriceAgreementAmount)
                                        ELSE
                                          NewPriceAgreementAmount := ROUND(NewPriceAgreementAmount, 0.01);
                                        IF UpdateByPrice THEN
                                          ContractAmountsbyDate.VALIDATE(Price, NewPriceAgreementAmount)
                                        ELSE BEGIN
                                          ContractAmountsbyDate.VALIDATE("Amount (LCY)", NewPriceAgreementAmount);
                                          ContractAmountsbyDate.UpdatePrice;
                                        END;
                                        IF Finalize THEN
                                          IF NOT ContractAmountsbyDate.INSERT(TRUE) THEN
                                            IF OverwriteExisting THEN
                                              ContractAmountsbyDate.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                        NewAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate."Amount (LCY)";
                                      END ELSE
                                        Msg := Text010;
                                    END ELSE
                                      IndexContractObjects(ContractObjectPriceAgreement, Msg);
                                  END;

                                  IF ShowErrors AND (Msg = '') THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Service Index Method;
               DataItemLink=Service Contract No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 2012;2   ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table11020322;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Service Contract No.,Employee No.,Starting Date)
                                 ORDER(Descending);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT UpdateCostPrices THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               SETRANGE("Starting Date", 0D, ReferenceDate);
                               LastServEmplCostPrice.INIT;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ServEmplCostPrice@1100528600 : Record 11020322;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF (LastServEmplCostPrice."Service Contract No." = "Service Contract No.") AND
                                     (LastServEmplCostPrice."Employee No." = "Employee No.")
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  Msg := '';

                                  ServEmplCostPrice := "Serv. - Empl. Cost Price";
                                  ServEmplCostPrice.SETRECFILTER;
                                  ServEmplCostPrice.SETFILTER("Starting Date", '>%1', NewIndexDate);
                                  IF NOT ServEmplCostPrice.ISEMPTY THEN
                                    Msg := Text002;

                                  NewPrice := ServEmplCostPrice."Cost Price";
                                  LastIndexDate := ServEmplCostPrice."Starting Date";
                                  ServEmplCostPrice.VALIDATE("Starting Date", NewIndexDate);
                                  ServEmplCostPrice.VALIDATE("Ending Date", 0D);
                                  ServEmplCostPrice.SETRECFILTER;
                                  IF NOT ServEmplCostPrice.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                                    ServEmplCostPrice.FINDFIRST;
                                    IF NOT OverwriteExisting THEN
                                      Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text009, TABLECAPTION, Text013)
                                    ELSE
                                      Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text009, TABLECAPTION, '');
                                  END;
                                  ServEmplCostPrice."Cost Price" *= (100 + CostPricePerc) / 100;
                                  IF RoundCostPrice <> 0 THEN
                                    ServEmplCostPrice."Cost Price" := ROUND(ServEmplCostPrice."Cost Price", RoundCostPrice)
                                  ELSE
                                    ServEmplCostPrice."Cost Price" := ROUND(ServEmplCostPrice."Cost Price", 0.01);
                                  NewPrice := ServEmplCostPrice."Cost Price";
                                  IF Finalize THEN
                                    IF NOT ServEmplCostPrice.INSERT(TRUE) THEN
                                      IF OverwriteExisting THEN
                                        ServEmplCostPrice.MODIFY(TRUE);

                                  LastServEmplCostPrice := "Serv. - Empl. Cost Price";

                                  IF ShowErrors AND (Msg = '') THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Service-Contract;
               DataItemLink=Service Contract No.=FIELD(No.) }

                                      Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text009, TABLECAPTION, '');
                                  END;
                                  ServCostObjectSalesPrice."Sales Price (LCY)" *= (100 + SalesPricePerc) / 100;
                                  IF RoundSalesPrice <> 0 THEN

                                  ELSE
                                    ServCostObjectSalesPrice."Sales Price (LCY)" := ROUND(ServCostObjectSalesPrice."Sales Price (LCY)", 0.01);
                                  ServCostObjectSalesPrice.VALIDATE("Sales Price (LCY)");
                                  NewPrice := ServCostObjectSalesPrice."Sales Price (LCY)";
                                  IF Finalize THEN
                                    IF NOT ServCostObjectSalesPrice.INSERT(TRUE) THEN
                                      IF OverwriteExisting THEN
                                        ServCostObjectSalesPrice.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                  LastServCostObjectSalesPrice := "Serv - Cost Object Sales Price";

                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

    { 5813;1   ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table11071928;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Service Contract No.,Index Date)
                                 ORDER(Descending);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT UpdateContractBudgetLines THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                               SETRANGE("Index Date", 0D, ReferenceDate);

                               IF RoundContractBudget = 0 THEN
                                 RoundContractBudget := 0.01;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SCBudgetVersionCalls@1100528600 : Record 11071928;
                                  ToSCBudgetVersionCalls@1100528604 : Record 11071928;
                                  FromSCBudgetLineVersionCalls@1100528601 : Record 11071929;
                                  ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls@1100528602 : Record 11071929;
                                  BudgetLineVersionInserted@1100528603 : Boolean;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF LastSCBudgetVersionCalls."Service Contract No." = "Service Contract No." THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  Msg := '';
                                  SCBudgetVersionCalls := "SC Budget Version - Calls";
                                  SCBudgetVersionCalls.SETRECFILTER;
                                  SCBudgetVersionCalls.SETFILTER("Index Date", '>%1', NewIndexDate);
                                  IF NOT SCBudgetVersionCalls.ISEMPTY THEN
                                    Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text002);
                                  SCBudgetVersionCalls.SETRANGE("Index Date", NewIndexDate);
                                  IF NOT SCBudgetVersionCalls.ISEMPTY THEN
                                    IF NOT OverwriteExisting THEN
                                      Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text009, TABLECAPTION, Text013)
                                    ELSE
                                      Msg := STRSUBSTNO(Text009, TABLECAPTION, '');

                                  IF Finalize THEN BEGIN
                                    SCBudgetVersionCalls."Index Date" := NewIndexDate;
                                    IF NOT SCBudgetVersionCalls.INSERT(TRUE) THEN
                                      IF OverwriteExisting AND ("Index Date" <> NewIndexDate) THEN
                                        IF ToSCBudgetVersionCalls.GET("Service Contract No.", NewIndexDate) THEN BEGIN
                                          ToSCBudgetVersionCalls.DELETE(TRUE);
                                          SCBudgetVersionCalls.INSERT(TRUE);
                                        END;

                                    FromSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.SETRANGE("Service Contract No.", "Service Contract No.");
                                    FromSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.SETRANGE("Index Date", "Index Date");
                                    IF FromSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.FINDSET THEN
                                      REPEAT
                                        ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls := FromSCBudgetLineVersionCalls;
                                        ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Index Date" := SCBudgetVersionCalls."Index Date";
                                        BudgetLineVersionInserted := ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.INSERT(TRUE);
                                        IF NOT BudgetLineVersionInserted THEN
                                          ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.FIND('=');

                                        CASE ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Type" OF
                                          ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Type"::Labor:
                                            BEGIN
                                              IF ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Rate Code" <> '' THEN
                                                ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.VALIDATE("Rate Code")
                                              ELSE BEGIN
                                                ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.Rate *= (100 + ContractBudgetLaborPerc) / 100;
                                                ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.Rate := ROUND(ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.Rate, RoundContractBudget);
                                                ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.VALIDATE(Rate);
                                              END;
                                            END;
                                        ELSE
                                          CASE ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Type" OF
                                            ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Type"::Material:
                                              ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Price" *= (100 + ContractBudgetMaterialPerc) / 100;
                                            ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Type"::Subcontracting:
                                              ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Price" *= (100 + ContractBudgetSubcontrPerc) / 100;
                                            ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Type"::Plant:
                                              ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Price" *= (100 + ContractBudgetPlantPerc) / 100;
                                            ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Type"::Sundry:
                                              ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Price" *= (100 + ContractBudgetSundryPerc) / 100;
                                          END;
                                          ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Price" := ROUND(ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls."Cost Price", RoundContractBudget);
                                          ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.VALIDATE("Cost Price");
                                        END;

                                        IF BudgetLineVersionInserted OR OverwriteExisting THEN
                                          ToSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                      UNTIL FromSCBudgetLineVersionCalls.NEXT = 0;
                                  END;
                                  LastSCBudgetVersionCalls := "SC Budget Version - Calls";

                                  IF ShowErrors AND (Msg = '') THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Service Contract No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100528600;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012828;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Service Contract No.,Service Package,Line No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT UpdateContractDiscountTerms THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ServiceContractDiscountTerm@1100528600 : Record 11012828;
                                BEGIN
                                  Msg := '';
                                  ServiceContractDiscountTerm := "Service Contract Discount Term";
                                  ServiceContractDiscountTerm."Service Contract No." := '';
                                  IF NOT ServiceContractDiscountTerm.FIND('=') THEN
                                    Msg := Text011
                                  ELSE BEGIN
                                    ServiceContractDiscountTerm."Service Contract No." := "Service Contract No.";
                                    ServiceContractDiscountTerm."Starting Date Discount" := "Starting Date Discount";
                                    IF FORMAT(ServiceContractDiscountTerm) <> FORMAT("Service Contract Discount Term") THEN
                                      Msg := Text012;
                                  END;

                                  IF ShowErrors AND (Msg = '') THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                END;

               OnPostDataItem=VAR
                                ServiceContractDiscountTerm@1100528600 : Record 11012828;
                                ContractObject@1100528602 : Record 11071702;
                              BEGIN
                                IF UpdateContractDiscountTerms AND Finalize THEN BEGIN
                                  ServiceContractDiscountTerm.SETRANGE("Service Contract No.", "Service-Contract"."No.");
                                  ServiceContractDiscountTerm.DELETEALL(TRUE);

                                  ContractObject.SETRANGE("Service Contract No.", "Service-Contract"."No.");
                                  IF ContractObject.FINDSET THEN
                                    REPEAT
                                      ContractObject.SetDoNotCreateMaintenanceLines(TRUE);
                                      ContractObject.VALIDATE("Service Package");
                                    UNTIL ContractObject.NEXT = 0;
                                END;
                              END;

               DataItemLink=Service Contract No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100528609;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11020344;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Entity Type,Entity Code,Line No.)
                                 WHERE(Entity Type=CONST(Service Contract));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT UpdateServiceExtraCost THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  Msg := '';
                                  NewPrice := Amount;
                                  CASE "Cost Type" OF
                                    "Cost Type"::Material:
                                      NewPrice *= (100 + ServiceExtraCostMaterialPerc) / 100;
                                    "Cost Type"::Labor:
                                      NewPrice *= (100 + ServiceExtraCostLaborPerc) / 100;
                                    "Cost Type"::Subcontracting:
                                      NewPrice *= (100 + ServiceExtraCostSubcontrPerc) / 100;
                                    "Cost Type"::Plant:
                                      NewPrice *= (100 + ServiceExtraCostPlantPerc) / 100;
                                    "Cost Type"::Sundry:
                                      NewPrice *= (100 + ServiceExtraCostSundryPerc) / 100;
                                  END;
                                  IF RoundServiceExtraCost <> 0 THEN
                                    NewPrice := ROUND(NewPrice, RoundServiceExtraCost)
                                  ELSE
                                    NewPrice := ROUND(NewPrice, 0.01);
                                  IF Finalize THEN BEGIN
                                    VALIDATE(Amount, NewPrice);
                                    MODIFY(TRUE);
                                  END;

                                  IF ShowErrors AND (Msg = '') THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Entity Code=FIELD(No.) }

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525000() : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525001() : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      EXIT("Maintenance Scheme Version".GETFILTERS);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE IndexContractObjects@1100528602(VAR IContractObject@1100528600 : Record 11071702;VAR OMsg@1100528900 : Text);
    VAR
      ContractAmountsbyDate@1100528602 : Record 11071708;
      NextIndexDate@1100528601 : Date;
      NewPriceAgreementAmount@1100528604 : Decimal;
      UpdateByPrice@1100528603 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF IContractObject."Last Index Date" <> 0D THEN
        LastIndexDate := IContractObject."Last Index Date"
      ELSE
        LastIndexDate := IContractObject."Index Starting Date";
      IF LastIndexDate = 0D THEN
        EXIT;
      IF LastIndexDate > NewIndexDate THEN
        EXIT;
      IF FORMAT(IContractObject."Index Interval") = '' THEN
        EXIT;
      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE(Type, ContractAmountsbyDate.Type::"Price Agreement");
      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Service Contract No.", IContractObject."Service Contract No.");
      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Service Object No.", IContractObject."Service Object No.");
      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETRANGE("Installment Line No.", 0);
      ContractAmountsbyDate.SETFILTER("Index Date", '<=%1', ReferenceDate);
      IF NOT ContractAmountsbyDate.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
        OMsg := Text010;
        EXIT;
      END;
      LastAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate."Amount (LCY)";
      NextIndexDate := LastIndexDate;

      WHILE CALCDATE(IContractObject."Index Interval", NextIndexDate) <= NewIndexDate DO
        NextIndexDate := CALCDATE(IContractObject."Index Interval", NextIndexDate);
      IF ContractAmountsbyDate.GET(
        ContractAmountsbyDate.Type::"Price Agreement", IContractObject."Service Contract No.", IContractObject."Service Object No.", 0, NextIndexDate)
      THEN
        IF OverwriteExisting THEN
          OMsg := STRSUBSTNO(Text014, '')
        ELSE
          OMsg := STRSUBSTNO(Text014, Text013);

      ContractAmountsbyDate."Index Date" := NextIndexDate;
      ContractAmountsbyDate.CALCFIELDS("Currency Code");
      UpdateByPrice := ContractAmountsbyDate.IsQuantityBasedOnContractObject AND (ContractAmountsbyDate."Currency Code" = '');
      IF UpdateByPrice THEN
        NewPriceAgreementAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate.Price * (100 + PriceAgreementAmountPerc) / 100
      ELSE
        NewPriceAgreementAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate."Amount (LCY)" * (100 + PriceAgreementAmountPerc) / 100;
      IF RoundPriceAgreementAmount <> 0 THEN
        NewPriceAgreementAmount := ROUND(NewPriceAgreementAmount, RoundPriceAgreementAmount)
      ELSE
        NewPriceAgreementAmount := ROUND(NewPriceAgreementAmount, 0.01);
      IF UpdateByPrice THEN
        ContractAmountsbyDate.VALIDATE(Price, NewPriceAgreementAmount)
      ELSE BEGIN
        ContractAmountsbyDate.VALIDATE("Amount (LCY)", NewPriceAgreementAmount);
        ContractAmountsbyDate.UpdatePrice;
      END;
      IF Finalize THEN BEGIN
        IF NOT ContractAmountsbyDate.INSERT(TRUE) THEN
          IF OverwriteExisting THEN
            ContractAmountsbyDate.MODIFY(TRUE);
        IContractObject."Last Index Date" := NextIndexDate;
        IContractObject.MODIFY;
        NewAmount := ContractAmountsbyDate."Amount (LCY)";
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SetServiceIndexByDateValues@1100529600();
    BEGIN
      ServiceIndexMethod := ServiceIndexByDate."Service Index Method";
      ServiceIndexDate := ServiceIndexByDate."Index Date";
      IF (ServiceIndexByDate."Service Index Method" = '') OR (ServiceIndexByDate."Index Date" = 0D) THEN
        EXIT;
      UpdateContractAmount := TRUE;
      ContractAmountPerc := ServiceIndexByDate."Index Percentage";
      RoundContractAmount := ServiceIndexByDate."Round Amount";
      UpdateInstallmentAmount := TRUE;
      InstallmentAmountPerc := ServiceIndexByDate."Index Percentage";
      RoundInstallmentAmount := ServiceIndexByDate."Round Amount";
      "Service-Contract".SETRANGE("Service Index Method", ServiceIndexMethod);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
